### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/proposal.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:07:43
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/proposal.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/proposal.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Why
2: 
3: When mimo-agent restarts, the ACP session is lost even though the chat history persists in mimo-platform. This causes the agent to lose conversation context, resulting in disjointed interactions where the AI behaves as if it's starting fresh. We need to connect mimo-platform sessions with ACP sessions so they share the same ID, and enable session resumption after agent restarts.
4: 
5: ## What Changes
6: 
7: - Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform session.yaml to persist ACP session references
8: - Extend WebSocket protocol to send `acpSessionId` from platform to agent on reconnection
9: - Add `acp_session_created` message from agent to report new/updated session IDs
10: - Implement capability-aware session resumption:
11:   - Check if ACP agent supports `loadSession` capability during initialization
12:   - If supported and `acpSessionId` exists: call `loadSession()` to resume conversation
13:   - If not supported or no session ID: create new session via `newSession()`
14: - Add transparent reset notification: when session cannot be resumed, append system message to chat history indicating the reset with timestamp
15: 
16: ## Capabilities
17: 
18: ### New Capabilities
19: - `session-acp-persistence`: Persist ACP session IDs in mimo-platform and enable session resumption across agent restarts
20: 
21: ### Modified Capabilities
22: - `agent-communication`: Extend WebSocket protocol with `acpSessionId` field in `session_ready` message and new `acp_session_created` message type
23: 
24: ## Impact
25: 
26: - **mimo-platform**: Session repository (YAML persistence), WebSocket handlers, chat service
27: - **mimo-agent**: AcpClient initialization logic, session management, WebSocket message handlers
28: - **User experience**: Seamless conversation continuity across agent restarts with clear notification when context is reset

(End of file - total 28 lines)
</content>
```

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:07:50
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## MODIFIED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: Agent connects successfully
4: The system SHALL allow agent to establish WebSocket connection and receive session information including ACP session ID.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Agent connects with valid token
7: - **WHEN** mimo-agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
8: - **AND** agent sends agent_ready message with {agentId, workdir}
9: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "online"
10: - **AND** system looks up all sessions assigned to agent
11: - **AND** system reads acpSessionId from each session's session.yaml
12: - **AND** system starts fossil server for each active session
13: - **AND** system sends session_ready message with {platformUrl, sessions: [{sessionId, port, checkoutPath, acpSessionId}]}
14: - **AND** system logs "Agent connected" to console
15: 
16: #### Scenario: Agent connects with multiple sessions
17: - **WHEN** agent connects with 3 assigned sessions
18: - **THEN** system starts 3 fossil servers on ports 8080, 8081, 8082
19: - **AND** system sends session_ready with all 3 sessions including acpSessionId for each
20: - **AND** agent clones all 3 checkouts
21: - **AND** agent spawns 3 ACP processes
22: 
23: #### Scenario: Agent handles session_ready
24: - **WHEN** agent receives session_ready message
25: - **THEN** agent parses each session in sessions array
26: - **AND** agent extracts acpSessionId from each session object
27: - **AND** agent computes absolute checkout path from relative path and workdir
28: - **AND** agent clones from fossilUrl to checkoutPath for each session
29: - **AND** agent spawns ACP process in each checkoutPath passing acpSessionId
30: - **AND** agent sends agent_sessions_ready to platform with {sessionIds: [...]}
31: 
32: ## ADDED Requirements
33: 
34: ### Requirement: Agent reports ACP session creation
35: The system SHALL receive acp_session_created message from agent after ACP session initialization.
36: 
37: #### Scenario: Agent creates new ACP session
38: - **WHEN** agent initializes ACP for a session
39: - **AND** agent either calls newSession() or loadSession()
40: - **THEN** agent sends acp_session_created to platform
41: - **AND** message contains {type: "acp_session_created", sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset}
42: - **AND** wasReset is true if newSession() was used when loadSession was possible
43: 
44: #### Scenario: Agent reports session resumption
45: - **WHEN** agent successfully calls loadSession() with existing acpSessionId
46: - **THEN** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: false
47: - **AND** chat history continues seamlessly without reset notification
48: 
49: ### Requirement: Agent handles ACP capability detection
50: The system SHALL detect ACP agent capabilities and choose appropriate session initialization method.
51: 
52: #### Scenario: ACP supports loadSession
53: - **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
54: - **AND** ACP initialize response has agentCapabilities.loadSession: true
55: - **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
56: - **THEN** agent calls connection.loadSession({sessionId: "acp-abc123", cwd, mcpServers})
57: - **AND** if successful, wasReset is false
58: - **AND** if fails, agent falls back to newSession() with wasReset: true
59: 
60: #### Scenario: ACP does not support loadSession
61: - **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
62: - **AND** ACP initialize response has agentCapabilities.loadSession: false or undefined
63: - **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
64: - **THEN** agent calls connection.newSession({cwd, mcpServers})
65: - **AND** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: true
66: - **AND** resetReason is "loadSession not supported"
67: 
68: #### Scenario: No persisted session ID
69: - **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
70: - **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: null
71: - **THEN** agent calls connection.newSession({cwd, mcpServers})
72: - **AND** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: false
73: - **AND** this is treated as initial session creation, not a reset

(End of file - total 73 lines)
</content>
```

<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/session-acp-persistence/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## ADDED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: Store ACP session ID in session.yaml
4: The system SHALL persist the ACP session identifier in the session's YAML configuration file.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: New ACP session created
7: - **WHEN** mimo-agent successfully creates a new ACP session via newSession()
8: - **AND** agent sends acp_session_created message to platform
9: - **THEN** platform stores the acpSessionId in session.yaml
10: - **AND** the field is named acpSessionId
11: - **AND** the value is the ACP session identifier string
12: 
13: #### Scenario: ACP session ID is optional
14: - **WHEN** loading a session from session.yaml
15: - **AND** the acpSessionId field is missing or null
16: - **THEN** system treats this as no persisted ACP session
17: - **AND** agent will create a new ACP session on next connection
18: 
19: ### Requirement: Send acpSessionId to agent on session_ready
20: The system SHALL include the persisted ACP session ID in the session_ready message sent to agents.
21: 
22: #### Scenario: Session with existing acpSessionId
23: - **WHEN** agent connects and system prepares session_ready message
24: - **AND** session has acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" in session.yaml
25: - **THEN** session_ready message includes acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
26: - **AND** the field is present in the session object within sessions array
27: 
28: #### Scenario: Session without acpSessionId
29: - **WHEN** agent connects and system prepares session_ready message
30: - **AND** session has no acpSessionId (null or missing)
31: - **THEN** session_ready message includes acpSessionId: null
32: - **AND** agent will create new ACP session
33: 
34: ### Requirement: Receive acp_session_created from agent
35: The system SHALL accept acp_session_created message from agent and update session.yaml.
36: 
37: #### Scenario: Agent reports new session
38: - **WHEN** agent sends acp_session_created message
39: - **AND** message contains {sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset, resetReason?}
40: - **THEN** platform updates session.yaml with new acpSessionId
41: - **AND** if wasReset is true, append system message to chat history
42: 
43: #### Scenario: Agent reports session resumption
44: - **WHEN** agent sends acp_session_created message
45: - **AND** wasReset is false
46: - **THEN** platform updates session.yaml with acpSessionId
47: - **AND** no system message is added to chat history
48: 
49: ### Requirement: Append system message on session reset
50: The system SHALL append a system message to chat.jsonl when ACP session cannot be resumed.
51: 
52: #### Scenario: Session reset with reason
53: - **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
54: - **AND** resetReason is "loadSession not supported"
55: - **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
56: - **AND** content includes timestamp and resetReason
57: - **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS (reason)"
58: 
59: #### Scenario: Session reset without specific reason
60: - **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
61: - **AND** no resetReason is provided
62: - **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
63: - **AND** content includes timestamp
64: - **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS"

(End of file - total 64 lines)
</content>

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:08:00)

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/design.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:08:01
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/design.md

````
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/design.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## Context
2: 
3: Currently, mimo-agent spawns a new ACP process for each user message, creating a fresh ACP session every time. When mimo-agent restarts (crash, redeploy, etc.), any in-memory state is lost. While mimo-platform persists chat history in `chat.jsonl`, the ACP session context (conversation state, model configuration, etc.) is completely reset.
4: 
5: The ACP protocol supports `loadSession()` for resuming existing sessions, but this capability:
6: 1. Is optional (agents advertise it via `agentCapabilities.loadSession`)
7: 2. Requires the client (mimo-agent) to persist the `acpSessionId` returned from `newSession()`
8: 
9: We need a mechanism to:
10: - Store ACP session IDs in mimo-platform (the source of truth for session state)
11: - Send the persisted ID to mimo-agent on reconnection
12: - Handle capability detection and graceful fallback
13: 
14: ## Goals / Non-Goals
15: 
16: **Goals:**
17: - Persist ACP session IDs in mimo-platform session storage
18: - Enable ACP session resumption when mimo-agent reconnects (if supported)
19: - Provide transparent session reset notification when resumption is not possible
20: - Maintain backward compatibility with ACP agents that don't support `loadSession`
21: 
22: **Non-Goals:**
23: - Changing the fundamental per-message ACP session lifecycle
24: - Persistent agent-side state (mimo-agent remains stateless)
25: - Automatic retry logic for failed `loadSession` calls
26: - Migration of existing sessions (they'll start fresh on next agent connect)
27: 
28: ## Decisions
29: 
30: ### Decision 1: Platform Owns Session Persistence
31: **Choice:** Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform's session.yaml, not in mimo-agent.
32: 
33: **Rationale:** 
34: - mimo-platform is the source of truth for session metadata
35: - mimo-agent is designed to be ephemeral/stateless
36: - Simplifies agent implementation - just receives the ID on connect
37: 
38: **Alternative:** Agent-side persistence (rejected): Would require agent to manage durable storage, complicating deployment and violating the stateless design.
39: 
40: ### Decision 2: Capability-Aware Resumption
41: **Choice:** Check `agentCapabilities.loadSession` and handle all cases explicitly.
42: 
43: **Rationale:**
44: - ACP spec marks `loadSession` as optional
45: - Graceful degradation provides better UX than hard failures
46: - Clear system messages keep users informed
47: 
48: **Flow:**
49: ```
50: Agent connects
51:     ↓
52: Initialize ACP connection
53:     ↓
54: Check capabilities
55:     ├─ loadSession=true AND acpSessionId exists → try loadSession()
56:     │   ├─ Success → session resumed
57:     │   └─ Failure → newSession() + reset notification
58:     └─ loadSession=false OR no acpSessionId → newSession() + reset notification
59: ```
60: 
61: ### Decision 3: Explicit Reset Notification
62: **Choice:** Append system message to chat.jsonl when session is reset.
63: 
64: **Rationale:**
65: - Users need visibility into when conversation context changes
66: - Timestamp provides audit trail
67: - Distinguishes between "resumed" (seamless) vs "reset" (new context)
68: 
69: **Message Format:**
70: ```json
71: {
72:   "role": "system",
73:   "content": "Session reset at 2026-04-07 15:30:45 (loadSession not supported)",
74:   "timestamp": "2026-04-07T15:30:45.000Z"
75: }
76: ```
77: 
78: ### Decision 4: Minimal WebSocket Protocol Extension
79: **Choice:** Add single field to existing `session_ready` message and single new message type `acp_session_created`.
80: 
81: **Rationale:**
82: - Minimizes changes to existing communication patterns
83: - `session_ready` already sends session configuration, natural place for acpSessionId
84: - `acp_session_created` provides clear lifecycle event
85: 
86: ## Risks / Trade-offs
87: 
88: | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
89: |------|-----------|--------|------------|
90: | `loadSession` fails silently | Low | Medium | Explicit error handling with fallback to newSession() |
91: | Stale acpSessionId causes errors | Low | Low | Catch loadSession errors, treat as new session |
92: | Chat history becomes confusing with resets | Medium | Low | Clear system messages with timestamps |
93: | ACP agent capabilities change between versions | Low | Low | Check capabilities on every connect, not cached |
94: 
95: **Trade-offs:**
96: - System messages add noise to chat history, but provide important context
97: - Additional YAML field increases storage slightly, but negligible impact
98: - Extra message roundtrip (acp_session_created) adds latency, but only on agent connect
99: 
100: ## Migration Plan
101: 
102: **Deployment:**
103: 1. Update mimo-platform to support new WebSocket protocol (backward compatible - acpSessionId is optional)
104: 2. Update mimo-agent to send/receive new message types
105: 3. Deploy mimo-platform
106: 4. Deploy mimo-agent
107: 
108: **Rollback:**
109: - Remove `acpSessionId` field from session.yaml (optional field, safe to ignore)
110: - Revert to previous agent version (will receive acpSessionId but ignore it, creating fresh sessions)
111: 
112: **Existing Sessions:**
113: - Sessions without `acpSessionId` will behave exactly as before (new ACP session each time)
114: - Field will be populated on first successful agent connection
115: 
116: ## Open Questions
117: 
118: None - design is ready for implementation.

(End of file - total 118 lines)
</content>
````

270:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
271:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
272:     }
273:   }
274: 
275:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
276:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
277: 
278:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
279:     
280:     for (const entry of entries) {
281:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
282:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
283:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
284:       } else {
285:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
286:       }
287:     }
288: 
289:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
290:   }
291: 
292:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
293:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
294:   }

<content>1: import { Agent, AgentRepository, AgentStatus, agentRepository } from "./repository.js";
2: import { SignJWT, jwtVerify } from "jose";
3: 
4: const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || "your-secret-key-change-in-production";
5: const AGENT_SECRET = new TextEncoder().encode(JWT_SECRET);
6: 
7: export interface AgentTokenPayload {
8:   agentId: string;
9:   sessionId?: string;
10:   projectId?: string;
11:   owner: string;
12: }
13: 
14: export interface CreateAgentInput {
15:   owner: string;
16:   sessionId?: string;
17:   projectId?: string;
18: }
19: 
20: export class AgentService {
21:   private activeConnections: Map<string, WebSocket> = new Map();
22:   private currentAcpRequest: Map<string, AbortController> = new Map();
23:   private agentWorkdirs: Map<string, string> = new Map();
24: 
25:   constructor(
26:     private repository: AgentRepository = agentRepository
27:   ) {}
28: 
29:   async createAgent(input: CreateAgentInput): Promise<Agent> {
30:     const agent = await this.repository.create({
31:       owner: input.owner,
32:     });
33: 
34:     const token = await this.generateAgentToken(agent, input.sessionId, input.projectId);
35:     await this.repository.update(agent.id, { token });
36:     
37:     return { ...agent, token };
38:   }
39: 
40:   async generateAgentToken(agent: Agent, sessionId?: string, projectId?: string): Promise<string> {
41:     const tokenPayload: any = {
42:       agentId: agent.id,
43:       owner: agent.owner,
44:     };
45:     
46:     if (sessionId) {
47:       tokenPayload.sessionId = sessionId;
48:     }
49:     if (projectId) {
50:       tokenPayload.projectId = projectId;
51:     }
52:     
53:     const token = await new SignJWT(tokenPayload)
54:       .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256" })
55:       .setIssuedAt()
56:       .setExpirationTime("1y")
57:       .sign(AGENT_SECRET);
58: 
59:     return token;
60:   }
61: 
62:   async verifyAgentToken(token: string): Promise<AgentTokenPayload | null> {
63:     try {
64:       const { payload } = await jwtVerify(token, AGENT_SECRET);
65:       return {
66:         agentId: payload.agentId as string,
67:         sessionId: payload.sessionId as string | undefined,
68:         projectId: payload.projectId as string | undefined,
69:         owner: payload.owner as string,
70:       };
71:     } catch (error) {
72:       console.error("[verifyAgentToken] Token verification failed:", error?.message || error);
73:       return null;
74:     }
75:   }
76: 
77:   async handleAgentConnect(agentId: string, ws: WebSocket, workdir?: string): Promise<void> {
78:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
79:     if (!agent) {
80:       ws.close(1008, "Agent not found");
81:       return;
82:     }
83: 
84:     this.activeConnections.set(agentId, ws);
85:     if (workdir) {
86:       this.agentWorkdirs.set(agentId, workdir);
87:     }
88:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "online");
89:     await this.repository.updateLastActivity(agentId);
90:   }
91: 
92:   getAgentWorkdir(agentId: string): string | undefined {
93:     return this.agentWorkdirs.get(agentId);
94:   }
95: 
96:   async handleAgentDisconnect(agentId: string): Promise<void> {
97:     this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
98:     await this.repository.updateStatus(agentId, "offline");
99:   }
100: 
101:   async cancelCurrentRequest(sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
102:     const sessionRepo = await import("../sessions/repository.js");
103:     const session = await sessionRepo.sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
104:     if (!session || !session.assignedAgentId) {
105:       return false;
106:     }
107: 
108:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(session.assignedAgentId);
109:     if (!agent || agent.status !== "online") {
110:       return false;
111:     }
112: 
113:     const controller = this.currentAcpRequest.get(session.assignedAgentId);
114:     if (controller) {
115:       controller.abort();
116:       this.currentAcpRequest.delete(session.assignedAgentId);
117:     }
118: 
119:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(session.assignedAgentId);
120:     if (ws) {
121:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "cancel_request" }));
122:     }
123: 
124:     return true;
125:   }
126: 
127:   async deleteAgent(agentId: string): Promise<boolean> {
128:     const agent = await this.repository.findById(agentId);
129:     if (!agent) return false;
130: 
131:     if (this.activeConnections.has(agentId)) {
132:       const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
133:       ws?.close(1000, "Agent deleted");
134:       this.activeConnections.delete(agentId);
135:     }
136: 
137:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
138:     await this.repository.delete(agentId);
139:     
140:     return true;
141:   }
142: 
143:   async getAgentStatus(agentId: string): Promise<Agent | null> {
144:     return this.repository.findById(agentId);
145:   }
146: 
147:   async listAgentsByOwner(owner: string): Promise<Agent[]> {
148:     return this.repository.findByOwner(owner);
149:   }
150: 
151:   async listAgentsByStatus(status: AgentStatus): Promise<Agent[]> {
152:     return this.repository.findByStatus(status);
153:   }
154: 
155:   isAgentOnline(agentId: string): boolean {
156:     return this.activeConnections.has(agentId);
157:   }
158: 
159:   getAgentConnection(agentId: string): WebSocket | undefined {
160:     return this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
161:   }
162: 
163:   startAcpRequest(agentId: string): AbortController {
164:     const controller = new AbortController();
165:     this.currentAcpRequest.set(agentId, controller);
166:     return controller;
167:   }
168: 
169:   endAcpRequest(agentId: string): void {
170:     this.currentAcpRequest.delete(agentId);
171:   }
172: 
173:   async sendToAgent(agentId: string, message: unknown): Promise<boolean> {
174:     const ws = this.activeConnections.get(agentId);
175:     if (!ws) return false;
176: 
177:     try {
178:       ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
179:       return true;
180:     } catch {
181:       return false;
182:     }
183:   }

<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/server.ts</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { spawn } from "child_process";
2: import { existsSync } from "fs";
3: 
4: interface RunningServer {
5:   process: ReturnType<typeof spawn>;
6:   port: number;
7:   repoPath: string;
8:   startTime: Date;
9: }
10: 
11: const runningServers: Map<number, RunningServer> = new Map();
12: let nextPort = 8000;
13: 
14: export function getNextPort(): number {
15:   const port = nextPort;
16:   nextPort++;
17:   if (nextPort > 9000) {
18:     nextPort = 8000; // Wrap around
19:   }
20:   return port;
21: }
22: 
23: export interface ServerResult {
24:   success: boolean;
25:   port?: number;
26:   error?: string;
27: }
28: 
29: export interface ServerInfo {
30:   port: number;
31:   repoPath: string;
32:   startTime: Date;
33: }
34: 
35: export const fossilServer = {
36:   start(repoPath: string, port: number = getNextPort()): Promise<ServerResult> {
37:     return new Promise((resolve) => {
38:       if (!existsSync(repoPath)) {
39:         resolve({
40:           success: false,
41:           error: `Repository not found: ${repoPath}`,
42:         });
43:         return;
44:       }
45: 
46:       // Check if port is already in use
47:       if (runningServers.has(port)) {
48:         resolve({
49:           success: false,
50:           error: `Port ${port} is already in use`,
51:         });
52:         return;
53:       }
54: 
55:       // Start fossil server
56:       const proc = spawn("fossil", ["server", repoPath, "--port", port.toString()], {
57:         stdio: ["ignore", "pipe", "pipe"],
58:         detached: false,
59:       });
60: 
61:       let started = false;
62:       let errorOutput = "";
63: 
64:       proc.stdout?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
65:         const output = data.toString();
66:         // Fossil server usually outputs something when it starts
67:         if (!started && output.includes("Listening") || output.includes("listening")) {
68:           started = true;
69:         }
70:       });
71: 
72:       proc.stderr?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
73:         errorOutput += data.toString();
74:       });
75: 
76:       proc.on("error", (err) => {
77:         if (!started) {
78:           resolve({
79:             success: false,
80:             error: err.message,
81:           });
82:         }
83:       });
84: 
85:       proc.on("exit", (code) => {
86:         runningServers.delete(port);
87:         if (!started) {
88:           resolve({
89:             success: false,
90:             error: errorOutput || `Server exited with code ${code}`,
91:           });
92:         }
93:       });
94: 
95:       // Give the server a moment to start
96:       setTimeout(() => {
97:         if (!started && proc.exitCode === null) {
98:           // Server is still running, assume it's started
99:           started = true;
100:         }
101: 
102:         if (started) {
103:           runningServers.set(port, {
104:             process: proc,
105:             port,
106:             repoPath,
107:             startTime: new Date(),
108:           });
109: 
110:           resolve({
111:             success: true,
112:             port,
113:           });
114:         } else {
115:           proc.kill();
116:           resolve({
117:             success: false,
118:             error: errorOutput || "Server failed to start",
119:           });
120:         }
121:       }, 500);
122:     });
123:   },
124: 
125:   stop(port: number): Promise<ServerResult> {
126:     return new Promise((resolve) => {
127:       const server = runningServers.get(port);
128:       if (!server) {
129:         resolve({
130:           success: false,
131:           error: `No server running on port ${port}`,
132:         });
133:         return;
134:       }
135: 
136:       server.process.kill();
137:       runningServers.delete(port);
138: 
139:       resolve({
140:         success: true,
141:         port,
142:       });
143:     });
144:   },
145: 
146:   isRunning(port: number): boolean {
147:     const server = runningServers.get(port);
148:     if (!server) return false;
149: 
150:     // Check if process is still alive
151:     return server.process.exitCode === null;
152:   },
153: 
154:   async healthCheck(port: number): Promise<boolean> {
155:     const server = runningServers.get(port);
156:     if (!server) return false;
157: 
158:     try {
159:       // Try to connect to the server
160:       const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:${port}`, {
161:         method: "GET",
162:       });
163:       return response.status === 200;
164:     } catch {
165:       return false;
166:     }
167:   },
168: 
169:   listRunning(): ServerInfo[] {
170:     const servers: ServerInfo[] = [];
171:     for (const [port, server] of runningServers) {
172:       if (this.isRunning(port)) {
173:         servers.push({
174:           port: server.port,
175:           repoPath: server.repoPath,
176:           startTime: server.startTime,
177:         });
178:       }
179:     }
180:     return servers;
181:   },
182: 
183:   stopAll(): Promise<void> {
184:     return new Promise((resolve) => {
185:       const promises = [];
186:       for (const [port] of runningServers) {
187:         promises.push(this.stop(port));
188:       }
189:       Promise.all(promises).then(() => resolve());
190:     });
191:   },
192: };
193: 
194: // Cleanup on process exit
195: process.on("exit", () => {
196:   fossilServer.stopAll();
197: });
198: 
199: process.on("SIGINT", () => {
200:   fossilServer.stopAll().then(() => {
201:     process.exit(0);
202:   });
203: });
204: 
205: process.on("SIGTERM", () => {
206:   fossilServer.stopAll().then(() => {
207:     process.exit(0);
208:   });
209: });

(End of file - total 209 lines)
</content>

<content>1: import * as acp from "@agentclientprotocol/sdk";
2: import { IAcpProvider, NewSessionResponse } from "./types";
3: import { ModelState, ModeState } from "../types";
4: 
5: export interface AcpClientCallbacks {
6:   onThoughtStart: (sessionId: string) => void;
7:   onThoughtChunk: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
8:   onThoughtEnd: (sessionId: string) => void;
9:   onMessageChunk: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
10:   onUsageUpdate: (sessionId: string, usage: any) => void;
11:   onGenericUpdate: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
12: }
13: 
14: export interface AcpClientSession {
15:   sessionId: string;
16:   acpSessionId: string;
17:   connection: acp.ClientSideConnection;
18:   modelState?: ModelState;
19:   modeState?: ModeState;
20:   currentThoughtBuffer?: string;
21: }
22: 
23: export class AcpClient {
24:   private provider: IAcpProvider;
25:   private sessionId: string;
26:   private callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks;
27:   private session: AcpClientSession | null = null;
28: 
29:   constructor(
30:     provider: IAcpProvider,
31:     sessionId: string,
32:     callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks
33:   ) {
34:     this.provider = provider;
35:     this.sessionId = sessionId;
36:     this.callbacks = callbacks;
37:   }
38: 
39:   get acpSessionId(): string | undefined {
40:     return this.session?.acpSessionId;
41:   }
42: 
43:   get modelState(): ModelState | undefined {
44:     return this.session?.modelState;
45:   }
46: 
47:   get modeState(): ModeState | undefined {
48:     return this.session?.modeState;
49:   }
50: 
51:   async initialize(
52:     cwd: string,
53:     input: WritableStream<Uint8Array>,
54:     output: ReadableStream<Uint8Array>
55:   ): Promise<NewSessionResponse> {
56:     const stream = acp.ndJsonStream(input, output);
57: 
58:     // Create client with update handlers
59:     const client: acp.Client = {
60:       requestPermission: async () => ({
61:         outcome: { outcome: "approved", options: ["allow"] },
62:       }),
63:       sessionUpdate: async (params) => {
64:         this.handleSessionUpdate(params.update as any);
65:       },
66:     };
67: 
68:     const connection = new acp.ClientSideConnection(() => client, stream);
69: 
70:     // Initialize connection
71:     const initResponse = await connection.initialize({
72:       protocolVersion: acp.PROTOCOL_VERSION,
73:       clientInfo: { name: "mimo-agent", version: "0.1.0" },
74:     });
75: 
76:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP initialized: ${initResponse.protocolVersion}`);
77: 
78:     // Create session
79:     const sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
80:       cwd,
81:       mcpServers: [],
82:     });
83: 
84:     // Extract state using provider
85:     const state = this.provider.extractState(
86:       sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse
87:     );
88: 
89:     // Store session info
90:     this.session = {
91:       sessionId: this.sessionId,
92:       acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,
93:       connection,
94:       modelState: state.modelState,
95:       modeState: state.modeState,
96:     };
97: 
98:     return sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse;
99:   }
100: 
101:   private handleSessionUpdate(update: any): void {
102:     const updateType = update?.sessionUpdate;
103: 
104:     if (!this.session) return;
105: 
106:     const mappedType = this.provider.mapUpdateType(updateType);
107: 
108:     // Skip updates we don't care about
109:     if (mappedType === null) return;
110: 
111:     switch (mappedType) {
112:       case "thought_chunk":
113:         // Send thought start on first chunk
114:         if (!this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
115:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
116:           this.callbacks.onThoughtStart(this.sessionId);
117:         }
118:         this.session.currentThoughtBuffer += update.content?.text || "";
119:         this.callbacks.onThoughtChunk(
120:           this.sessionId,
121:           update.content?.text || ""
122:         );
123:         break;
124: 
125:       case "message_chunk":
126:         // End thought buffering if active
127:         if (this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
128:           this.callbacks.onThoughtEnd(this.sessionId);
129:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
130:         }
131:         this.callbacks.onMessageChunk(
132:           this.sessionId,
133:           update.content?.text || ""
134:         );
135:         break;
136: 
137:       case "usage_update":
138:         this.callbacks.onUsageUpdate(this.sessionId, {
139:           cost: update.cost || {},
140:           size: update.size,
141:           used: update.used,
142:         });
143:         break;
144: 
145:       default:
146:         this.callbacks.onGenericUpdate(this.sessionId, updateType || "update");
147:     }
148:   }
149: 
150:   async prompt(content: string): Promise<acp.PromptResponse> {
151:     if (!this.session) {
152:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
153:     }
154: 
155:     return this.session.connection.prompt({
156:       sessionId: this.session.acpSessionId,
157:       prompt: [{ type: "text", text: content }],
158:     });
159:   }
160: 
161:   async setModel(modelId: string): Promise<void> {
162:     if (!this.session) {
163:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
164:     }
165: 
166:     if (!this.session.modelState) {
167:       throw new Error("Model state not available");
168:     }
169: 
170:     await this.provider.setModel(
171:       this.session.connection,
172:       this.session.acpSessionId,
173:       modelId,
174:       this.session.modelState.optionId
175:     );
176: 
177:     // Update local state
178:     this.session.modelState.currentModelId = modelId;
179:   }
180: 
181:   async setMode(modeId: string): Promise<void> {
182:     if (!this.session) {
183:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
184:     }
185: 
186:     if (!this.session.modeState) {
187:       throw new Error("Mode state not available");
188:     }
189: 
190:     await this.provider.setMode(
191:       this.session.connection,
192:       this.session.acpSessionId,
193:       modeId,
194:       this.session.modeState.optionId
195:     );
196: 
197:     // Update local state
198:     this.session.modeState.currentModeId = modeId;
199:   }
200: }

82: import configRoutes from "./config/routes";
83: app.route("/config", configRoutes);
84: 
85: // Credentials routes (protected)
86: import credentialsRoutes from "./credentials/routes";
87: app.route("/credentials", credentialsRoutes);
88: 
89: // Health check
90: app.get("/health", (c) => {
91:   console.log("Health check hit");
92:   return c.json({ status: "healthy" });
93: });
94: 
95: // 404 handler
96: app.notFound((c) => {
97:   console.log(`404: ${c.req.url}`);
98:   return c.json({ error: "Not Found", path: c.req.path }, 404);
99: });
100: 
101: const server = Bun.serve({
102:   async fetch(req: Request, server: any) {
103:     const url = new URL(req.url);
104:     
105:     // Handle WebSocket upgrade requests
106:     if (req.headers.get("upgrade") === "websocket") {
107:       const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/agent or /ws/chat
108:       
109:       if (type === 'agent') {
110:         const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
111:         if (!token) {
112:           console.log("[WS] Missing token");
113:           return new Response("Missing token", { status: 400 });
114:         }
115:         
116:         const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
117:         if (!payload) {
118:           console.log("[WS] Invalid token");
119:           return new Response("Invalid token", { status: 401 });
120:         }
121:         
122:         console.log("[WS] Token verified, agentId:", payload.agentId);
123:         
124:         const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
125:           data: {
126:             connectionType: 'agent',
127:             agentId: payload.agentId,
128:             url: req.url
129:           }
130:         });
131:         
132:         if (!upgraded) {
133:           console.log("[WS] WebSocket upgrade failed");
134:           return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
135:         }
136:         console.log("[WS] WebSocket upgraded successfully for agent:", payload.agentId);
137:         return undefined;
138:       }
139:       
140:       if (type === 'chat') {
141:         const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
142:         if (!sessionId) {
143:           return new Response("Missing sessionId", { status: 400 });
144:         }
145:         
146:         const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
147:           data: {
148:             connectionType: 'chat',
149:             sessionId,
150:             url: req.url
151:           }
152:         });
153:         
154:         if (!upgraded) {
155:           return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
156:         }
157:         return undefined;
158:       }
159:       
160:       return new Response("Unknown WebSocket endpoint", { status: 404 });
161:     }
162:     
163:     return app.fetch(req);
164:   },
165:   port: PORT,
166:   websocket: {
167:     // WebSocket handler for different connection types
168:     async message(ws, message) {
169:       try {
170:         const data = JSON.parse(message as string);
171:         const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
172:         
173:         switch (connectionType) {
174:           case 'agent':
175:             await handleAgentMessage(ws, data);
176:             break;
177:           case 'chat':
178:             await handleChatMessage(ws, data);
179:             break;
180:           default:
181:             console.log("Unknown connection type");
182:         }
183:       } catch (error) {
184:         console.error("WebSocket message error:", error);
185:       }
186:     },
187:     async open(ws) {
188:       const url = new URL(ws.data.url);
189:       const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/chat or /ws/agent
190:       
191:       if (type === 'chat') {
192:         // Chat connection
193:         const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
194:         ws.data.connectionType = 'chat';
195:         ws.data.sessionId = sessionId;
196:         
197:         // Add to session subscribers
198:         if (!chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
199:           chatSessions.set(sessionId, new Set());
200:         }
201:         chatSessions.get(sessionId).add(ws);
202:         
203:         // Send chat history
204:         const history = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
205:         ws.send(JSON.stringify({
206:           type: 'history',
207:           messages: history,
208:         }));
209:         
210:         console.log(`Chat client connected to session ${sessionId}`);
211:       } else {
212:         // Agent connection
213:         const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
214:         
215:         if (!token) {
216:           ws.close(1008, "Missing token");
217:           return;
218:         }
219: 
220:         const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
221:         if (!payload) {
222:           ws.close(1008, "Invalid token");
223:           return;
224:         }
225: 
226:         ws.data.connectionType = 'agent';
227:         ws.data.agentId = payload.agentId;
228:         ws.data.authenticated = true;  // Mark as authenticated, waiting for agent_ready
229:         
230:         await agentService.handleAgentConnect(payload.agentId, ws);
231:         console.log(`Agent ${payload.agentId} connected, waiting for agent_ready`);
232:       }
233:     },
234:     async close(ws) {
235:       const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
236:       
237:       if (connectionType === 'chat') {
238:         // Remove from session subscribers
239:         const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
240:         if (chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
241:           chatSessions.get(sessionId).delete(ws);
242:           if (chatSessions.get(sessionId).size === 0) {
243:             chatSessions.delete(sessionId);
244:           }
245:         }
246:         console.log(`Chat client disconnected from session ${sessionId}`);
247:       } else if (connectionType === 'agent') {
248:         const agentId = ws.data.agentId;
249:         if (agentId) {
250:           await agentService.handleAgentDisconnect(agentId);
251:           console.log(`Agent ${agentId} disconnected`);
252: 
253:           // Stop Fossil servers for assigned sessions after grace period
254:           const agent = await agentRepository.findById(agentId);
255:           if (agent && agent.sessionIds && agent.sessionIds.length > 0) {
256:             // 30-second grace period for unexpected disconnects
257:             setTimeout(async () => {
258:               // Check if agent reconnected
259:               if (!agentService.isAgentOnline(agentId)) {
260:                 // Agent didn't reconnect, stop all servers
261:                 for (const sessionId of agent.sessionIds) {
262:                   if (fossilServerManager.isServerRunning(sessionId)) {
263:                     await fossilServerManager.stopServer(sessionId);
264:                     console.log(`Stopped Fossil server for session ${sessionId}`);
265:                   }
266:                 }
267:               }
268:             }, 30000);
269:           }
270:         }
271:       }
272:     },
273:   },
274: });
275: 
276: // Handle agent messages
277: async function handleAgentMessage(ws, data) {
278:   console.log("[agent] Received message:", data.type, data);
279:   process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
280:   
281:   switch (data.type) {
282:     case "ping":
283:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "pong" }));
284:       break;
285:     case "agent_ready":
286:       console.log("[agent] Agent ready:", data.agentId, "workdir:", data.workdir);
287:       process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
288:       
289:       // Store workdir for relative path computation
290:       const agentId = ws.data.agentId;
291:       if (data.workdir) {
292:         agentService.handleAgentConnect(agentId, ws, data.workdir);
293:       }
294:       
295:       // Start Fossil servers for sessions assigned to this agent
296:       // Note: Sessions are assigned via assignedAgentId, not in agent.sessionIds
297:       const sessions = await sessionRepository.findByAssignedAgentId(agentId);
298:       console.log("[agent] Found", sessions.length, "sessions assigned to agent", agentId);
299:       process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
300:       
301:       if (sessions.length > 0) {
302:         const sessionsReady = [];
303:         const workdir = agentService.getAgentWorkdir(agentId);
304:         console.log("[agent] Workdir:", workdir);
305:         process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
306:         
307:         for (const session of sessions) {
308:           const sessionId = session.id;
309:           console.log("[agent] Session:", sessionId, "status:", session.status);
310:           process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
311:           
312:           if (session.status === "active") {
313:             const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
314:             console.log("[agent] Starting fossil server for session:", sessionId, "fossil:", fossilPath);
315:             process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
316:             
317:             const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer(sessionId, fossilPath);
318:             console.log("[agent] Fossil server result:", result);
319:             process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
320:             
321:             if ('port' in result) {
322:               // Update session with port
323:               await sessionRepository.update(sessionId, { port: result.port });
324:               
325:               // Get session with credentials
326:               const sessionWithCreds = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
327:               
328:               sessionsReady.push({
329:                 sessionId,
330:                 port: result.port,
331:                 agentWorkspaceUser: sessionWithCreds?.agentWorkspaceUser,
332:                 agentWorkspacePassword: sessionWithCreds?.agentWorkspacePassword,
333:               });
334:             } else {
335:               console.error("[agent] Failed to start fossil server:", result.error);
336:             }
337:           }
338:         }
339:         
340:         // Send session_ready message to agent
341:         if (sessionsReady.length > 0) {
342:           const message = {
343:             type: 'session_ready',
344:             platformUrl: `http://localhost:${PORT}`,
345:             sessions: sessionsReady,
346:           };
347:           console.log("[agent] Sending session_ready:", JSON.stringify(message));
348:           process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
349:           ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
350:         } else {
351:           console.log("[agent] No sessions ready to send");
352:         }
353:       } else {
354:         console.log("[agent] No sessions assigned to agent");
355:       }
356:       break;
357:     case "thought_start":
358:       {
359:         const startSessionId = data.sessionId;
360:         if (!startSessionId) {
361:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_start");
362:           return;
363:         }
364:         
365:         // Start new thought buffer
366:         thoughtBuffers.set(startSessionId, "");
367:         
368:         // Forward to clients
369:         const subscribers = chatSessions.get(startSessionId);
370:         if (subscribers) {
371:           subscribers.forEach(client => {
372:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
373:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
374:                 type: data.type,
375:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
376:               }));
377:             }
378:           });
379:         }
380:       }
381:       break;
382:       
383:     case "thought_chunk":
384:       {
385:         const chunkSessionId = data.sessionId;
386:         if (!chunkSessionId) {
387:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_chunk");
388:           return;
389:         }
390:         
391:         // Accumulate thought chunks
392:         const currentThoughtBuffer = thoughtBuffers.get(chunkSessionId) || "";
393:         thoughtBuffers.set(chunkSessionId, currentThoughtBuffer + (data.content || ""));
394:         
395:         // Forward to clients
396:         const thoughtChunkSubscribers = chatSessions.get(chunkSessionId);
397:         if (thoughtChunkSubscribers) {
398:           thoughtChunkSubscribers.forEach(client => {
399:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
400:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
401:                 type: data.type,
402:                 content: data.content,
403:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
404:               }));
405:             }
406:           });
407:         }
408:       }
409:       break;
410:       
411:     case "thought_end":
412:       {
413:         const endSessionId = data.sessionId;
414:         if (!endSessionId) {
415:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_end");
416:           return;
417:         }
418:         
419:         // Forward to clients
420:         const endSubscribers = chatSessions.get(endSessionId);
421:         if (endSubscribers) {
422:           endSubscribers.forEach(client => {
423:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
424:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
425:                 type: data.type,
426:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
427:               }));
428:             }
429:           });
430:         }
431:       }
432:       break;
433:       
434:     case "message_chunk":
435:       {
436:         const msgSessionId = data.sessionId;
437:         if (!msgSessionId) {
438:           console.log("No sessionId in message_chunk");
439:           return;
440:         }
441:         
442:         // Accumulate message chunks
443:         const currentBuffer = streamingBuffers.get(msgSessionId) || "";
444:         streamingBuffers.set(msgSessionId, currentBuffer + (data.content || ""));
445:         
446:         // Forward to clients
447:         const msgSubscribers = chatSessions.get(msgSessionId);
448:         if (msgSubscribers) {
449:           msgSubscribers.forEach(client => {
450:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
451:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
452:                 type: data.type,
453:                 content: data.content,
454:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
455:               }));
456:             }
457:           });
458:         }
459:       }
460:       break;
461:       
462:     case "usage_update":
463:       {
464:         const usageSessionId = data.sessionId;
465:         if (!usageSessionId) {
466:           console.log("No sessionId in usage_update");
467:           return;
468:         }
469:         
470:         // Get accumulated message and thoughts
471:         const messageContent = streamingBuffers.get(usageSessionId);
472:         const thoughtContent = thoughtBuffers.get(usageSessionId);
473:         
474:         if (messageContent || thoughtContent) {
475:           // Save assistant response with optional thoughts
476:           let fullContent = messageContent || "";
477:           
478:           // Prepend thoughts if present
479:           if (thoughtContent) {
480:             fullContent = `<details><summary>Thought Process</summary>${thoughtContent}</details>\n\n${fullContent}`;
481:             thoughtBuffers.delete(usageSessionId);
482:           }
483:           
484:           await chatService.saveMessage(usageSessionId, {
485:             role: "assistant",
486:             content: fullContent,
487:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
488:           });
489:           
490:           // Clear buffer
491:           streamingBuffers.delete(usageSessionId);
492:         }
493:         
494:         // Forward usage update to clients
495:         const usageSubscribers = chatSessions.get(usageSessionId);
496:         if (usageSubscribers) {
497:           usageSubscribers.forEach(client => {
498:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
499:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
500:                 type: data.type,
501:                 usage: data.usage,
502:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
503:               }));
504:             }
505:           });
506:         }
507:       }
508:       break;
509:     
510:     case "acp_response":
511:       // Legacy: Handle simple ACP response and broadcast to chat
512:       // Agent must specify which session this is for
513:       const sessionId = data.sessionId;
514:       if (!sessionId) {
515:         console.log("No sessionId in acp_response");
516:         return;
517:       }
518:       
519:       // Broadcast to all chat clients in session
520:       const subscribers = chatSessions.get(sessionId);
521:       if (subscribers) {
522:         subscribers.forEach(client => {
523:           if (client.readyState === 1) { // WebSocket.OPEN
524:             client.send(JSON.stringify({
525:               type: 'message',
526:               role: 'assistant',
527:               content: data.content,
528:               timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
529:             }));
530:           }
531:         });
532:       }
533:       
534:       // Save to history
535:       await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
536:         role: 'assistant',
537:         content: data.content,
538:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
539:       });
540:       break;
541:     case "file_changed":
542:       console.log("File changed:", data.files);
543:       
544:       const fileSessionId = data.sessionId;
545:       if (!fileSessionId) {
546:         console.log("No sessionId in file_changed");
547:         return;
548:       }
549:       
550:       const changes = data.files.map((file) => ({
551:         path: file.path,
552:         isNew: file.isNew,
553:         deleted: file.deleted,
554:       }));
555:       
556:       await fileSyncService.initializeSession(fileSessionId, "", "");
557:       await fileSyncService.handleFileChanges(fileSessionId, changes);
558:       break;
559:     case "session_error":
560:       console.log("[agent] Session error:", data.sessionId, data.error);
561:       break;
562:     case "agent_sessions_ready":
563:       console.log("[agent] Agent sessions ready:", data.sessionIds);
564:       break;
565:     case "session_initialized":
566:       // Store model/mode state from agent
567:       if (data.sessionId) {
568:         if (data.modelState) {
569:           sessionStateService.setModelState(data.sessionId, data.modelState);
570:           console.log(`[agent] Session ${data.sessionId} model state:`, data.modelState.currentModelId);
571:         }
572:         if (data.modeState) {
573:           sessionStateService.setModeState(data.sessionId, data.modeState);
574:           console.log(`[agent] Session ${data.sessionId} mode state:`, data.modeState.currentModeId);
575:         }
576:         
577:         // Broadcast to chat clients
578:         const initSubscribers = chatSessions.get(data.sessionId);
579:         if (initSubscribers) {
580:           const initMessage: any = {
581:             type: 'session_initialized',
582:             sessionId: data.sessionId,
583:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
584:           };
585:           if (data.modelState) {
586:             initMessage.modelState = data.modelState;
587:           }
588:           if (data.modeState) {
589:             initMessage.modeState = data.modeState;
590:           }
591:           
592:           initSubscribers.forEach((client: WebSocket) => {
593:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
594:               client.send(JSON.stringify(initMessage));
595:             }
596:           });
597:         }
598:       }
599:       break;
600:     case "model_state":
601:       // Update and broadcast model state
602:       if (data.sessionId && data.modelState) {
603:         sessionStateService.setModelState(data.sessionId, data.modelState);
604:         
605:         const modelSubscribers = chatSessions.get(data.sessionId);
606:         if (modelSubscribers) {
607:           modelSubscribers.forEach((client: WebSocket) => {
608:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
609:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
610:                 type: 'model_state',
611:                 sessionId: data.sessionId,
612:                 modelState: data.modelState,
613:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
614:               }));
615:             }
616:           });
617:         }
618:       }
619:       break;
620:     case "mode_state":
621:       // Update and broadcast mode state
622:       if (data.sessionId && data.modeState) {
623:         sessionStateService.setModeState(data.sessionId, data.modeState);
624:         
625:         const modeSubscribers = chatSessions.get(data.sessionId);
626:         if (modeSubscribers) {
627:           modeSubscribers.forEach((client: WebSocket) => {
628:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
629:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
630:                 type: 'mode_state',
631:                 sessionId: data.sessionId,
632:                 modeState: data.modeState,
633:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
634:               }));
635:             }
636:           });
637:         }
638:       }
639:       break;
640:     default:
641:       console.log("[agent] Unknown message type:", data.type);
642:   }
643: }
644: 
645: // Handle chat messages
646: async function handleChatMessage(ws, data) {
647:   const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
648:   
649:   switch (data.type) {
650:     case "send_message":
651:       // Save user message
652:       await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
653:         role: 'user',
654:         content: data.content,
655:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
656:       });
657: 
658:       // Broadcast to all clients in session
659:       const subscribers = chatSessions.get(sessionId);
660:       if (subscribers) {
661:         subscribers.forEach(client => {
662:           if (client.readyState === 1) {
663:             client.send(JSON.stringify({
664:               type: 'message',
665:               role: 'user',
666:               content: data.content,
667:               timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
668:             }));
669:           }
670:         });
671:       }
672: 
673:       // Get session to find assigned agent
674:       const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
675:       if (session?.assignedAgentId) {
676:         // Forward to agent if connected
677:         const ws = agentService.getAgentConnection(session.assignedAgentId);
678:         if (ws && ws.readyState === 1) {
679:           ws.send(JSON.stringify({
680:             type: 'user_message',
681:             sessionId: sessionId,
682:             content: data.content,
683:           }));
684:         }
685:       }
686:       break;
687: 
688:     case "set_model":
689:       // Forward model change to agent
690:       const modelSession = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
691:       if (modelSession?.assignedAgentId) {
692:         const agentWs = agentService.getAgentConnection(modelSession.assignedAgentId);
693:         if (agentWs && agentWs.readyState === 1) {
694:           agentWs.send(JSON.stringify({
695:             type: 'set_model',
696:             sessionId: sessionId,
697:             modelId: data.modelId,
698:           }));
699:         }
700:       }
701:       break;
702: 
703:     case "set_mode":
704:       // Forward mode change to agent
705:       const modeSession = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
706:       if (modeSession?.assignedAgentId) {
707:         const modeAgentWs = agentService.getAgentConnection(modeSession.assignedAgentId);
708:         if (modeAgentWs && modeAgentWs.readyState === 1) {
709:           modeAgentWs.send(JSON.stringify({
710:             type: 'set_mode',
711:             sessionId: sessionId,
712:             modeId: data.modeId,
713:           }));
714:         }
715:       }
716:       break;
717: 
718:     case "request_state":
719:       // Forward state request to agent
720:       const stateSession = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
721:       if (stateSession?.assignedAgentId) {
722:         const stateAgentWs = agentService.getAgentConnection(stateSession.assignedAgentId);
723:         if (stateAgentWs && stateAgentWs.readyState === 1) {
724:           stateAgentWs.send(JSON.stringify({
725:             type: 'request_state',
726:             sessionId: sessionId,
727:           }));
728:         }
729:       }
730:       break;
731:       
732:     case "request_replay":
733:       const history = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
734:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({
735:         type: 'history',
736:         messages: history,
737:       }));
738:       break;
739:       
740:     default:
741:       console.log("Unknown chat message type:", data.type);
742:   }
743: }
744: 
745: // Server is ready
746: console.log(`Server running at http://localhost:${server.port}`);

(End of file - total 746 lines)
</content>

3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: 
5: export interface ChatMessage {
6:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
7:   content: string;
8:   timestamp: string;
9:   metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
10: }
11: 
12: export class ChatService {
13:   private getChatPath(sessionId: string): string {
14:     // Store chat in the session directory
15:     const Paths = getPaths();
16:     const sessionDir = this.findSessionDir(sessionId);
17:     if (!sessionDir) {
18:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
19:     }
20:     return join(sessionDir, "chat.jsonl");
21:   }
22: 
23:   private findSessionDir(sessionId: string): string | null {
24:     const Paths = getPaths();
25:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
26:       return null;
27:     }
28: 
29:     const { readdirSync } = require("fs");
30:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
31:     
32:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
33:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
34:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
35:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
36:           const sessionDir = join(sessionsDir, sessionId);
37:           if (existsSync(sessionDir)) {
38:             return sessionDir;
39:           }
40:         }
41:       }
42:     }
43: 
44:     return null;
45:   }
46: 
47:   async saveMessage(sessionId: string, message: ChatMessage): Promise<void> {
48:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
49:     const line = JSON.stringify(message) + "\n";
50:     appendFileSync(chatPath, line, "utf-8");
51:   }
52: 
53:   async loadHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<ChatMessage[]> {
54:     try {
55:       const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
56:       if (!existsSync(chatPath)) {
57:         return [];
58:       }
59: 
60:       const content = readFileSync(chatPath, "utf-8");
61:       const lines = content.trim().split("\n").filter(line => line);
62:       
63:       return lines.map((line) => JSON.parse(line) as ChatMessage);
64:     } catch {
65:       return [];
66:     }
67:   }
68: 
69:   async appendToHistory(sessionId: string, messages: ChatMessage[]): Promise<void> {
70:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
71:     const lines = messages.map((msg) => JSON.stringify(msg)).join("\n") + "\n";
72:     appendFileSync(chatPath, lines, "utf-8");
73:   }
74: 
75:   async clearHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
76:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
77:     if (existsSync(chatPath)) {
78:       const { unlinkSync } = require("fs");
79:       unlinkSync(chatPath);
80:     }
81:   }
82: }
83: 
84: export const chatService = new ChatService();

(End of file - total 84 lines)
</content>

5: 
6: export class OpencodeProvider implements IAcpProvider {
7:   readonly name = "opencode";
8: 
9:   spawn(cwd: string): {
10:     process: ChildProcess;
11:     stdin: Writable;
12:     stdout: Readable;
13:     stderr?: Readable;
14:   } {
15:     const proc = spawn("opencode", ["acp"], {
16:       cwd,
17:       stdio: ["pipe", "pipe", "pipe"],
18:     });
19: 
20:     return {
21:       process: proc,
22:       stdin: proc.stdin!,
23:       stdout: proc.stdout!,
24:       stderr: proc.stderr!,
25:     };
26:   }
27: 
28:   extractState(
29:     response: NewSessionResponse
30:   ): {
31:     modelState?: ModelState;
32:     modeState?: ModeState;
33:   } {
34:     const result: { modelState?: ModelState; modeState?: ModeState } = {};
35: 
36:     // Try modern configOptions first
37:     if (response.configOptions) {
38:       const modelConfig = response.configOptions.find(
39:         (opt) => opt.category === "model" && opt.type === "select"
40:       );
41:       const modeConfig = response.configOptions.find(
42:         (opt) => opt.category === "mode" && opt.type === "select"
43:       );
44: 
45:       if (modelConfig && modelConfig.type === "select") {
46:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modelConfig.options)
47:           ? modelConfig.options.map((opt) => ({
48:               value: opt.value,
49:               name: opt.name,
50:               description: opt.description,
51:             }))
52:           : [];
53: 
54:         result.modelState = {
55:           currentModelId: modelConfig.currentValue || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
56:           availableModels: availableOptions,
57:           optionId: modelConfig.id,
58:         };
59:       }
60: 
61:       if (modeConfig && modeConfig.type === "select") {
62:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modeConfig.options)
63:           ? modeConfig.options.map((opt) => ({
64:               value: opt.value,
65:               name: opt.name,
66:               description: opt.description,
67:             }))
68:           : [];
69: 
70:         result.modeState = {
71:           currentModeId: modeConfig.currentValue || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
72:           availableModes: availableOptions,
73:           optionId: modeConfig.id,
74:         };
75:       }
76:     }
77:     // Fallback to legacy format (models/modes fields)
78:     else if (response.models) {
79:       // Extract model state from legacy 'models' field
80:       if (response.models) {
81:         const models = response.models;
82:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(models.availableModels)
83:           ? models.availableModels.map((m) => ({
84:               value: m.modelId || m.id || "",
85:               name: m.name || m.modelId || m.id || "",
86:               description: m.description,
87:             }))
88:           : [];
89: 
90:         result.modelState = {
91:           currentModelId: models.currentModelId || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
92:           availableModels: availableOptions,
93:           optionId: "model",
94:         };
95:       }
96: 
97:       // Extract mode state from legacy 'modes' field
98:       if (response.modes) {
99:         const modes = response.modes;
100:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modes.availableModes)
101:           ? modes.availableModes.map((m) => ({
102:               value: m.id,
103:               name: m.name || m.id,
104:               description: m.description,
105:             }))
106:           : [];
107: 
108:         result.modeState = {
109:           currentModeId: modes.currentModeId || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
110:           availableModes: availableOptions,
111:           optionId: "mode",
112:         };
113:       }
114:     }
115: 
116:     return result;
117:   }
118: 
119:   async setModel(
120:     connection: any,
121:     acpSessionId: string,
122:     modelId: string,
123:     optionId: string
124:   ): Promise<void> {
125:     // Opencode doesn't support setSessionConfigOption, always use extMethod
126:     await connection.extMethod("session/set_model", {
127:       sessionId: acpSessionId,
128:       modelId: modelId,
129:     });
130:   }
131: 
132:   async setMode(
133:     connection: any,
134:     acpSessionId: string,
135:     modeId: string,
136:     optionId: string
137:   ): Promise<void> {
138:     // Opencode doesn't support setSessionConfigOption, always use extMethod
139:     // Note: opencode expects "modeId", not "mode"
140:     await connection.extMethod("session/set_mode", {
141:       sessionId: acpSessionId,
142:       modeId: modeId,
143:     });
144:   }
145: 
146:   mapUpdateType(updateType: string): string | null {
147:     const mapping: Record<string, string | null> = {
148:       agent_thought_chunk: "thought_chunk",
149:       agent_message_chunk: "message_chunk",
150:       usage_update: "usage_update",
151:       available_commands_update: null, // Skip
152:     };
153: 
154:     // Only handle known update types - skip unknown ones (like available_commands_update)
155:     return mapping[updateType] ?? null;
156:   }
157: }

(End of file - total 157 lines)

106:      * - Listen for connection closure: `connection.signal.addEventListener('abort', () => {...})`
107:      * - Check connection status synchronously: `if (connection.signal.aborted) {...}`
108:      * - Pass to other APIs (fetch, setTimeout) for automatic cancellation

136:      *
