391:      * This method handles the whole lifecycle of a prompt:
392:      * - Receives user messages with optional context (files, images, etc.)
393:      * - Processes the prompt using language models
394:      * - Reports language model content and tool calls to the Clients
395:      * - Requests permission to run tools
396:      * - Executes any requested tool calls
397:      * - Returns when the turn is complete with a stop reason
398:      *
399:      * See protocol docs: [Prompt Turn](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn)
400:      */
401:     prompt(params: schema.PromptRequest): Promise<schema.PromptResponse>;
402:     /**
403:      * Cancels ongoing operations for a session.
404:      *
405:      * This is a notification sent by the client to cancel an ongoing prompt turn.
406:      *
407:      * Upon receiving this notification, the Agent SHOULD:
408:      * - Stop all language model requests as soon as possible
409:      * - Abort all tool call invocations in progress
410:      * - Send any pending `session/update` notifications
411:      * - Respond to the original `session/prompt` request with `StopReason::Cancelled`
412:      *
413:      * See protocol docs: [Cancellation](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn#cancellation)
414:      */
415:     cancel(params: schema.CancelNotification): Promise<void>;
416:     /**
417:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
418:      *
419:      * Starts a NES (Next Edit Suggestions) session.
420:      *
421:      * @experimental
422:      */
423:     unstable_startNes(params: schema.StartNesRequest): Promise<schema.StartNesResponse>;
424:     /**
425:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
426:      *
427:      * Sends a NES suggestion request.
428:      *
429:      * @experimental
430:      */
431:     unstable_suggestNes(params: schema.SuggestNesRequest): Promise<schema.SuggestNesResponse>;
432:     /**
433:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
434:      *
435:      * Closes a NES session.
436:      *
437:      * @experimental
438:      */
439:     unstable_closeNes(params: schema.CloseNesRequest): Promise<schema.CloseNesResponse>;
440:     /**
441:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
442:      *
443:      * Notifies the agent that a document was opened.
444:      *
445:      * @experimental
446:      */
447:     unstable_didOpenDocument(params: schema.DidOpenDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
448:     /**
449:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
450:      *
451:      * Notifies the agent that a document was changed.
452:      *
453:      * @experimental
454:      */
455:     unstable_didChangeDocument(params: schema.DidChangeDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
456:     /**
457:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
458:      *
459:      * Notifies the agent that a document was closed.
460:      *
461:      * @experimental
462:      */
463:     unstable_didCloseDocument(params: schema.DidCloseDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
464:     /**
465:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
466:      *
467:      * Notifies the agent that a document was saved.
468:      *
469:      * @experimental
470:      */
471:     unstable_didSaveDocument(params: schema.DidSaveDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
472:     /**
473:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
474:      *
475:      * Notifies the agent that a document received focus.
476:      *
477:      * @experimental
478:      */
479:     unstable_didFocusDocument(params: schema.DidFocusDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
480:     /**
481:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
482:      *
483:      * Notifies the agent that a NES suggestion was accepted.
484:      *
485:      * @experimental
486:      */
487:     unstable_acceptNes(params: schema.AcceptNesNotification): Promise<void>;
488:     /**
489:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
490:      *
491:      * Notifies the agent that a NES suggestion was rejected.
492:      *
493:      * @experimental
494:      */
495:     unstable_rejectNes(params: schema.RejectNesNotification): Promise<void>;
496:     /**
497:      * Extension method
498:      *
499:      * Allows the Client to send an arbitrary request that is not part of the ACP spec.
500:      */
501:     extMethod(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<Record<string, unknown>>;
502:     /**
503:      * Extension notification
504:      *
505:      * Allows the Client to send an arbitrary notification that is not part of the ACP spec.
506:      */
507:     extNotification(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void>;
508:     /**
509:      * AbortSignal that aborts when the connection closes.
510:      *
511:      * This signal can be used to:
512:      * - Listen for connection closure: `connection.signal.addEventListener('abort', () => {...})`
513:      * - Check connection status synchronously: `if (connection.signal.aborted) {...}`
514:      * - Pass to other APIs (fetch, setTimeout) for automatic cancellation
515:      *
516:      * The connection closes when the underlying stream ends, either normally or due to an error.
517:      *
518:      * @example
519:      * ```typescript
520:      * const connection = new ClientSideConnection(client, stream);
521:      *
522:      * // Listen for closure
523:      * connection.signal.addEventListener('abort', () => {
524:      *   console.log('Connection closed - performing cleanup');
525:      * });
526:      *
527:      * // Check status
528:      * if (connection.signal.aborted) {
529:      *   console.log('Connection is already closed');
530:      * }
531:      *
532:      * // Pass to other APIs
533:      * fetch(url, { signal: connection.signal });
534:      * ```
535:      */
536:     get signal(): AbortSignal;
537:     /**
538:      * Promise that resolves when the connection closes.
539:      *
540:      * The connection closes when the underlying stream ends, either normally or due to an error.
541:      * Once closed, the connection cannot send or receive any more messages.
542:      *
543:      * This is useful for async/await style cleanup:
544:      *
545:      * @example
546:      * ```typescript
547:      * const connection = new ClientSideConnection(client, stream);
548:      * await connection.closed;
549:      * console.log('Connection closed - performing cleanup');
550:      * ```
551:      */
552:     get closed(): Promise<void>;
553: }
554: export type { AnyMessage } from "./jsonrpc.js";
555: declare class Connection {
556:     #private;
557:     constructor(requestHandler: RequestHandler, notificationHandler: NotificationHandler, stream: Stream);
558:     /**
559:      * AbortSignal that aborts when the connection closes.
560:      *
561:      * This signal can be used to:
562:      * - Listen for connection closure via event listeners
563:      * - Check connection status synchronously with `signal.aborted`
564:      * - Pass to other APIs (fetch, setTimeout) for automatic cancellation
565:      */
566:     get signal(): AbortSignal;
567:     /**
568:      * Promise that resolves when the connection closes.
569:      *
570:      * The connection closes when the underlying stream ends, either normally
571:      * or due to an error. Once closed, the connection cannot send or receive
572:      * any more messages.
573:      *
574:      * @example
575:      * ```typescript
576:      * const connection = new ClientSideConnection(client, stream);
577:      * await connection.closed;
578:      * console.log('Connection closed - performing cleanup');
579:      * ```
580:      */
581:     get closed(): Promise<void>;
582:     sendRequest<Req, Resp>(method: string, params?: Req): Promise<Resp>;
583:     sendNotification<N>(method: string, params?: N): Promise<void>;
584: }
585: /**
586:  * JSON-RPC error object.
587:  *
588:  * Represents an error that occurred during method execution, following the
589:  * JSON-RPC 2.0 error object specification with optional additional data.
590:  *
591:  * See protocol docs: [JSON-RPC Error Object](https://www.jsonrpc.org/specification#error_object)
592:  */
593: export declare class RequestError extends Error {
594:     code: number;
595:     data?: unknown;
596:     constructor(code: number, message: string, data?: unknown);
597:     /**
598:      * Invalid JSON was received by the server. An error occurred on the server while parsing the JSON text.
599:      */
600:     static parseError(data?: unknown, additionalMessage?: string): RequestError;
601:     /**
602:      * The JSON sent is not a valid Request object.
603:      */
604:     static invalidRequest(data?: unknown, additionalMessage?: string): RequestError;
605:     /**
606:      * The method does not exist / is not available.
607:      */
608:     static methodNotFound(method: string): RequestError;
609:     /**
610:      * Invalid method parameter(s).
611:      */
612:     static invalidParams(data?: unknown, additionalMessage?: string): RequestError;
613:     /**
614:      * Internal JSON-RPC error.
615:      */
616:     static internalError(data?: unknown, additionalMessage?: string): RequestError;
617:     /**
618:      * Authentication required.
619:      */
620:     static authRequired(data?: unknown, additionalMessage?: string): RequestError;
621:     /**
622:      * Resource, such as a file, was not found
623:      */
624:     static resourceNotFound(uri?: string): RequestError;
625:     toResult<T>(): Result<T>;
626:     toErrorResponse(): ErrorResponse;
627: }
628: /**
629:  * The Client interface defines the interface that ACP-compliant clients must implement.
630:  *
631:  * Clients are typically code editors (IDEs, text editors) that provide the interface
632:  * between users and AI agents. They manage the environment, handle user interactions,
633:  * and control access to resources.
634:  */
635: export interface Client {
636:     /**
637:      * Requests permission from the user for a tool call operation.
638:      *
639:      * Called by the agent when it needs user authorization before executing
640:      * a potentially sensitive operation. The client should present the options
641:      * to the user and return their decision.
642:      *
643:      * If the client cancels the prompt turn via `session/cancel`, it MUST
644:      * respond to this request with `RequestPermissionOutcome::Cancelled`.
645:      *
646:      * See protocol docs: [Requesting Permission](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/tool-calls#requesting-permission)
647:      */
648:     requestPermission(params: schema.RequestPermissionRequest): Promise<schema.RequestPermissionResponse>;
649:     /**
650:      * Handles session update notifications from the agent.
651:      *
652:      * This is a notification endpoint (no response expected) that receives
653:      * real-time updates about session progress, including message chunks,
654:      * tool calls, and execution plans.
655:      *
656:      * Note: Clients SHOULD continue accepting tool call updates even after
657:      * sending a `session/cancel` notification, as the agent may send final
658:      * updates before responding with the cancelled stop reason.
659:      *
660:      * See protocol docs: [Agent Reports Output](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn#3-agent-reports-output)
661:      */
662:     sessionUpdate(params: schema.SessionNotification): Promise<void>;
663:     /**
664:      * Writes content to a text file in the client's file system.
665:      *
666:      * Only available if the client advertises the `fs.writeTextFile` capability.
667:      * Allows the agent to create or modify files within the client's environment.
668:      *
669:      * See protocol docs: [Client](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#client)
670:      */
671:     writeTextFile?(params: schema.WriteTextFileRequest): Promise<schema.WriteTextFileResponse>;
672:     /**
673:      * Reads content from a text file in the client's file system.
674:      *
675:      * Only available if the client advertises the `fs.readTextFile` capability.
676:      * Allows the agent to access file contents within the client's environment.
677:      *
678:      * See protocol docs: [Client](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#client)
679:      */
680:     readTextFile?(params: schema.ReadTextFileRequest): Promise<schema.ReadTextFileResponse>;
681:     /**
682:      * Creates a new terminal to execute a command.
683:      *
684:      * Only available if the `terminal` capability is set to `true`.
685:      *
686:      * The Agent must call `releaseTerminal` when done with the terminal
687:      * to free resources.
688:   
689:      * @see {@link https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/terminals | Terminal Documentation}
690:      */
691:     createTerminal?(params: schema.CreateTerminalRequest): Promise<schema.CreateTerminalResponse>;
692:     /**
693:      * Gets the current output and exit status of a terminal.
694:      *
695:      * Returns immediately without waiting for the command to complete.
696:      * If the command has already exited, the exit status is included.
697:      *
698:      * @see {@link https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/terminals#getting-output | Getting Terminal Output}
699:      */
700:     terminalOutput?(params: schema.TerminalOutputRequest): Promise<schema.TerminalOutputResponse>;
701:     /**
702:      * Releases a terminal and frees all associated resources.
703:      *
704:      * The command is killed if it hasn't exited yet. After release,
705:      * the terminal ID becomes invalid for all other terminal methods.
706:      *
707:      * Tool calls that already contain the terminal ID continue to
708:      * display its output.
709:      *
710:      * @see {@link https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/terminals#releasing-terminals | Releasing Terminals}
711:      */
712:     releaseTerminal?(params: schema.ReleaseTerminalRequest): Promise<schema.ReleaseTerminalResponse | void>;
713:     /**
714:      * Waits for a terminal command to exit and returns its exit status.
715:      *
716:      * This method returns once the command completes, providing the
717:      * exit code and/or signal that terminated the process.
718:      *
719:      * @see {@link https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/terminals#waiting-for-exit | Waiting for Exit}
720:      */
721:     waitForTerminalExit?(params: schema.WaitForTerminalExitRequest): Promise<schema.WaitForTerminalExitResponse>;
722:     /**
723:      * Kills a terminal command without releasing the terminal.
724:      *
725:      * While `releaseTerminal` also kills the command, this method keeps
726:      * the terminal ID valid so it can be used with other methods.
727:      *
728:      * Useful for implementing command timeouts that terminate the command
729:      * and then retrieve the final output.
730:      *
731:      * Note: Call `releaseTerminal` when the terminal is no longer needed.
732:      *
733:      * @see {@link https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/terminals#killing-commands | Killing Commands}
734:      */
735:     killTerminal?(params: schema.KillTerminalRequest): Promise<schema.KillTerminalResponse | void>;
736:     /**
737:      * Extension method
738:      *
739:      * Allows the Agent to send an arbitrary request that is not part of the ACP spec.
740:      *
741:      * To help avoid conflicts, it's a good practice to prefix extension
742:      * methods with a unique identifier such as domain name.
743:      */
744:     extMethod?(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<Record<string, unknown>>;
745:     /**
746:      * Extension notification
747:      *
748:      * Allows the Agent to send an arbitrary notification that is not part of the ACP spec.
749:      */
750:     extNotification?(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void>;
751: }
752: /**
753:  * The Agent interface defines the interface that all ACP-compliant agents must implement.
754:  *
755:  * Agents are programs that use generative AI to autonomously modify code. They handle
756:  * requests from clients and execute tasks using language models and tools.
757:  */
758: export interface Agent {
759:     /**
760:      * Establishes the connection with a client and negotiates protocol capabilities.
761:      *
762:      * This method is called once at the beginning of the connection to:
763:      * - Negotiate the protocol version to use
764:      * - Exchange capability information between client and agent
765:      * - Determine available authentication methods
766:      *
767:      * The agent should respond with its supported protocol version and capabilities.
768:      *
769:      * See protocol docs: [Initialization](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/initialization)
770:      */
771:     initialize(params: schema.InitializeRequest): Promise<schema.InitializeResponse>;
772:     /**
773:      * Creates a new conversation session with the agent.
774:      *
775:      * Sessions represent independent conversation contexts with their own history and state.
776:      *
777:      * The agent should:
778:      * - Create a new session context
779:      * - Connect to any specified MCP servers
780:      * - Return a unique session ID for future requests
781:      *
782:      * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to expand the session's filesystem
783:      * scope beyond `cwd` without changing the base for relative paths.
784:      *
785:      * May return an `auth_required` error if the agent requires authentication.
786:      *
787:      * See protocol docs: [Session Setup](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/session-setup)
788:      */
789:     newSession(params: schema.NewSessionRequest): Promise<schema.NewSessionResponse>;
790:     /**
791:      * Loads an existing session to resume a previous conversation.
792:      *
793:      * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `loadSession` capability.
794:      *
795:      * The agent should:
796:      * - Restore the session context and conversation history
797:      * - Connect to the specified MCP servers
798:      * - Stream the entire conversation history back to the client via notifications
799:      *
800:      * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to set the complete list of
801:      * additional workspace roots for the loaded session.
802:      *
803:      * See protocol docs: [Loading Sessions](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/session-setup#loading-sessions)
804:      */
805:     loadSession?(params: schema.LoadSessionRequest): Promise<schema.LoadSessionResponse>;
806:     /**
807:      * **UNSTABLE**
808:      *
809:      * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
810:      *
811:      * Forks an existing session to create a new independent session.
812:      *
813:      * Creates a new session based on the context of an existing one, allowing
814:      * operations like generating summaries without affecting the original session's history.
815:      *
816:      * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to set the complete list of
817:      * additional workspace roots for the forked session.
818:      *
819:      * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `session.fork` capability.
820:      *
821:      * @experimental
822:      */
823:     unstable_forkSession?(params: schema.ForkSessionRequest): Promise<schema.ForkSessionResponse>;
824:     /**
825:      * Lists existing sessions from the agent.
826:      *
827:      * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `listSessions` capability.
828:      *
829:      * Returns a list of sessions with metadata like session ID, working directory,
830:      * title, and last update time. Supports filtering by working directory,
831:      * `additionalDirectories`, and cursor-based pagination.
832:      */
833:     listSessions?(params: schema.ListSessionsRequest): Promise<schema.ListSessionsResponse>;
834:     /**
835:      * **UNSTABLE**
836:      *
837:      * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
838:      *
839:      * Resumes an existing session without returning previous messages.
840:      *
841:      * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `session.resume` capability.
842:      *
843:      * The agent should resume the session context, allowing the conversation to continue
844:      * without replaying the message history (unlike `session/load`).
845:      *
846:      * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to set the complete list of
847:      * additional workspace roots for the resumed session.
848:      *
849:      * @experimental
850:      */
851:     unstable_resumeSession?(params: schema.ResumeSessionRequest): Promise<schema.ResumeSessionResponse>;
852:     /**
853:      * **UNSTABLE**
854:      *
855:      * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
856:      *
857:      * Closes an active session and frees up any resources associated with it.
858:      *
859:      * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `session.close` capability.
860:      *
861:      * The agent must cancel any ongoing work (as if `session/cancel` was called)
862:      * and then free up any resources associated with the session.
863:      *
864:      * @experimental
865:      */
866:     unstable_closeSession?(params: schema.CloseSessionRequest): Promise<schema.CloseSessionResponse>;
867:     /**
868:      * Sets the operational mode for a session.
869:      *
870:      * Allows switching between different agent modes (e.g., "ask", "architect", "code")
871:      * that affect system prompts, tool availability, and permission behaviors.
872:      *
873:      * The mode must be one of the modes advertised in `availableModes` during session
874:      * creation or loading. Agents may also change modes autonomously and notify the
875:      * client via `current_mode_update` notifications.
876:      *
877:      * This method can be called at any time during a session, whether the Agent is
878:      * idle or actively generating a turn.
879:      *
880:      * See protocol docs: [Session Modes](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/session-modes)
881:      */
882:     setSessionMode?(params: schema.SetSessionModeRequest): Promise<schema.SetSessionModeResponse | void>;
883:     /**
884:      * **UNSTABLE**
885:      *
886:      * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
887:      *
888:      * Select a model for a given session.
889:      *
890:      * @experimental
891:      */
892:     unstable_setSessionModel?(params: schema.SetSessionModelRequest): Promise<schema.SetSessionModelResponse | void>;
893:     /**
894:      * Set a configuration option for a given session.
895:      *
896:      * The response contains the full set of configuration options and their current values,
897:      * as changing one option may affect the available values or state of other options.
898:      */
899:     setSessionConfigOption?(params: schema.SetSessionConfigOptionRequest): Promise<schema.SetSessionConfigOptionResponse>;
900:     /**
901:      * Authenticates the client using the specified authentication method.
902:      *
903:      * Called when the agent requires authentication before allowing session creation.
904:      * The client provides the authentication method ID that was advertised during initialization.
905:      *
906:      * After successful authentication, the client can proceed to create sessions with
907:      * `newSession` without receiving an `auth_required` error.
908:      *
909:      * See protocol docs: [Initialization](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/initialization)
910:      */
911:     authenticate(params: schema.AuthenticateRequest): Promise<schema.AuthenticateResponse | void>;
912:     /**
913:      * Terminates the current authenticated session.
914:      *
915:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
916:      *
917:      * @experimental
918:      */
919:     unstable_logout?(params: schema.LogoutRequest): Promise<schema.LogoutResponse | void>;
920:     /**
921:      * Processes a user prompt within a session.
922:      *
923:      * This method handles the whole lifecycle of a prompt:
924:      * - Receives user messages with optional context (files, images, etc.)
925:      * - Processes the prompt using language models
926:      * - Reports language model content and tool calls to the Clients
927:      * - Requests permission to run tools
928:      * - Executes any requested tool calls
929:      * - Returns when the turn is complete with a stop reason
930:      *
931:      * See protocol docs: [Prompt Turn](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn)
932:      */
933:     prompt(params: schema.PromptRequest): Promise<schema.PromptResponse>;
934:     /**
935:      * Cancels ongoing operations for a session.
936:      *
937:      * This is a notification sent by the client to cancel an ongoing prompt turn.
938:      *
939:      * Upon receiving this notification, the Agent SHOULD:
940:      * - Stop all language model requests as soon as possible
941:      * - Abort all tool call invocations in progress
942:      * - Send any pending `session/update` notifications
943:      * - Respond to the original `session/prompt` request with `StopReason::Cancelled`
944:      *
945:      * See protocol docs: [Cancellation](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn#cancellation)
946:      */
947:     cancel(params: schema.CancelNotification): Promise<void>;
948:     /**
949:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
950:      *
951:      * Starts a NES (Next Edit Suggestions) session.
952:      *
953:      * @experimental
954:      */
955:     unstable_startNes?(params: schema.StartNesRequest): Promise<schema.StartNesResponse>;
956:     /**
957:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
958:      *
959:      * Sends a NES suggestion request.
960:      *
961:      * @experimental
962:      */
963:     unstable_suggestNes?(params: schema.SuggestNesRequest): Promise<schema.SuggestNesResponse>;
964:     /**
965:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
966:      *
967:      * Closes a NES session.
968:      *
969:      * @experimental
970:      */
971:     unstable_closeNes?(params: schema.CloseNesRequest): Promise<schema.CloseNesResponse | void>;
972:     /**
973:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
974:      *
975:      * Called when a document is opened.
976:      *
977:      * @experimental
978:      */
979:     unstable_didOpenDocument?(params: schema.DidOpenDocumentNotification): Promise<void>;
980:     /**
981:      * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
982:      *
983:      * Called when a document is changed.
984:      *

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:12:06)

I see from line 273 that `loadSession` is a method on `ClientSideConnection`. But looking at line 805, `loadSession?` is optional on the `Agent` interface (meaning it's only available if the agent advertises the `loadSession` capability).

So the flow is:
- Agent side implements the `Agent` interface (line 758)
- The `Agent` interface has `loadSession?` as an optional method (line 805)
- If the agent supports `loadSession`, it advertises this capability during initialization

Looking at the code flow, the ACP agent (opencode) is the "Agent" in this context, and mimo-agent is the "Client" that connects to it. So mimo-agent calls `connection.loadSession()` if the agent supports it.

Let me look at the schema types to see the InitializeResponse to understand how capabilities are exchanged.

90:     this.session = {
91:       sessionId: this.sessionId,
92:       acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,

95:       modeState: state.modeState,
96:     };
97: 
98:     return sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse;
99:   }
100: 
101:   private handleSessionUpdate(update: any): void {
102:     const updateType = update?.sessionUpdate;
103: 
104:     if (!this.session) return;
105: 
106:     const mappedType = this.provider.mapUpdateType(updateType);
107: 
108:     // Skip updates we don't care about
109:     if (mappedType === null) return;
110: 
111:     switch (mappedType) {
112:       case "thought_chunk":
113:         // Send thought start on first chunk
114:         if (!this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
115:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
116:           this.callbacks.onThoughtStart(this.sessionId);
117:         }
118:         this.session.currentThoughtBuffer += update.content?.text || "";
119:         this.callbacks.onThoughtChunk(
120:           this.sessionId,
121:           update.content?.text || ""
122:         );
123:         break;
124: 
125:       case "message_chunk":
126:         // End thought buffering if active
127:         if (this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
128:           this.callbacks.onThoughtEnd(this.sessionId);
129:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
130:         }
131:         this.callbacks.onMessageChunk(
132:           this.sessionId,
133:           update.content?.text || ""
134:         );
135:         break;
136: 
137:       case "usage_update":
138:         this.callbacks.onUsageUpdate(this.sessionId, {
139:           cost: update.cost || {},
140:           size: update.size,
141:           used: update.used,
142:         });
143:         break;
144: 
145:       default:
146:         this.callbacks.onGenericUpdate(this.sessionId, updateType || "update");
147:     }
148:   }
149: 
150:   async prompt(content: string): Promise<acp.PromptResponse> {
151:     if (!this.session) {
152:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
153:     }
154: 
155:     return this.session.connection.prompt({
156:       sessionId: this.session.acpSessionId,
157:       prompt: [{ type: "text", text: content }],
158:     });
159:   }
160: 
161:   async setModel(modelId: string): Promise<void> {
162:     if (!this.session) {
163:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
164:     }
165: 
166:     if (!this.session.modelState) {
167:       throw new Error("Model state not available");
168:     }
169: 
170:     await this.provider.setModel(
171:       this.session.connection,
172:       this.session.acpSessionId,
173:       modelId,
174:       this.session.modelState.optionId
175:     );
176: 
177:     // Update local state
178:     this.session.modelState.currentModelId = modelId;
179:   }
180: 
181:   async setMode(modeId: string): Promise<void> {
182:     if (!this.session) {

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-agent/src/acp/client.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:12:55
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/src/acp/client.ts
newString: export class AcpClient {
  private provider: IAcpProvider;
  private sessionId: string;
  private callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks;
  private session: AcpClientSession | null = null;
  private capabilities: { loadSession?: boolean } = {};

  constructor(
    provider: IAcpProvider,
    sessionId: string,
    callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks
  ) {
    this.provider = provider;
    this.sessionId = sessionId;
    this.callbacks = callbacks;
  }

  get acpSessionId(): string | undefined {
    return this.session?.acpSessionId;
  }

  get modelState(): ModelState | undefined {
    return this.session?.modelState;
  }

  get modeState(): ModeState | undefined {
    return this.session?.modeState;
  }

  async initialize(
    cwd: string,
    input: WritableStream<Uint8Array>,
    output: ReadableStream<Uint8Array>,
    existingSessionId?: string
  ): Promise<InitializeResult> {
    const stream = acp.ndJsonStream(input, output);

    const client: acp.Client = {
      requestPermission: async () => ({
        outcome: { outcome: "approved", options: ["allow"] },
      }),
      sessionUpdate: async (params) => {
        this.handleSessionUpdate(params.update as any);
      },
    };

    const connection = new acp.ClientSideConnection(() => client, stream);

    const initResponse = await connection.initialize({
      protocolVersion: acp.PROTOCOL_VERSION,
      clientInfo: { name: "mimo-agent", version: "0.1.0" },
    });

    console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP initialized: ${initResponse.protocolVersion}`);

    this.capabilities = {
      loadSession: initResponse.agentCapabilities?.loadSession ?? false,
    };
    console.log(`[mimo-agent] Agent capabilities:`, this.capabilities);

    let sessionResponse: acp.NewSessionResponse;
    let wasReset = false;
    let resetReason: string | undefined;

    if (existingSessionId && this.capabilities.loadSession) {
      try {
        console.log(`[mimo-agent] Attempting to load existing session: ${existingSessionId}`);
        sessionResponse = await connection.loadSession({
          sessionId: existingSessionId,
          cwd,
          mcpServers: [],
        });
        console.log(`[mimo-agent] Session loaded successfully: ${sessionResponse.sessionId}`);
      } catch (error) {
        console.log(`[mimo-agent] Failed to load session, creating new session:`, error);
        wasReset = true;
        resetReason = "loadSession failed";
        sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
          cwd,
          mcpServers: [],
        });
      }
    } else {
      if (existingSessionId && !this.capabilities.loadSession) {
        wasReset = true;
        resetReason = "loadSession not supported";
      }
      sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
        cwd,
        mcpServers: [],
      });
    }

    const state = this.provider.extractState(
      sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse
    );

    this.session = {
      sessionId: this.sessionId,
      acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,
      connection,
      modelState: state.modelState,
      modeState: state.modeState,
    };

    return {
      acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,
      wasReset,
      resetReason,
    };
  }

  async loadSession(
    cwd: string,
    input: WritableStream<Uint8Array>,
    output: ReadableStream<Uint8Array>,
    sessionId: string
  ): Promise<InitializeResult> {
    return this.initialize(cwd, input, output, sessionId);
  }
oldString: export class AcpClient {
  private provider: IAcpProvider;
  private sessionId: string;
  private callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks;
  private session: AcpClientSession | null = null;

  constructor(
    provider: IAcpProvider,
    sessionId: string,
    callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks
  ) {
    this.provider = provider;
    this.sessionId = sessionId;
    this.callbacks = callbacks;
  }

  get acpSessionId(): string | undefined {
    return this.session?.acpSessionId;
  }

  get modelState(): ModelState | undefined {
    return this.session?.modelState;
  }

  get modeState(): ModeState | undefined {
    return this.session?.modeState;
  }

  async initialize(
    cwd: string,
    input: WritableStream<Uint8Array>,
    output: ReadableStream<Uint8Array>
  ): Promise<NewSessionResponse> {
    const stream = acp.ndJsonStream(input, output);

    // Create client with update handlers
    const client: acp.Client = {
      requestPermission: async () => ({
        outcome: { outcome: "approved", options: ["allow"] },
      }),
      sessionUpdate: async (params) => {
        this.handleSessionUpdate(params.update as any);
      },
    };

    const connection = new acp.ClientSideConnection(() => client, stream);

    // Initialize connection
    const initResponse = await connection.initialize({
      protocolVersion: acp.PROTOCOL_VERSION,
      clientInfo: { name: "mimo-agent", version: "0.1.0" },
    });

    console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP initialized: ${initResponse.protocolVersion}`);

    // Create session
    const sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
      cwd,
      mcpServers: [],
    });

    // Extract state using provider
    const state = this.provider.extractState(
      sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse
    );

    // Store session info
    this.session = {
      sessionId: this.sessionId,
      acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,
      connection,
      modelState: state.modelState,
      modeState: state.modeState,
    };

    return sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse;
  }

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-agent/src/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:13:31
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/src/index.ts
newString:   private async handleSessionReady(message: any): Promise<void> {
    const { platformUrl, sessions } = message;

    if (!sessions || sessions.length === 0) {
      console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessions assigned");
      return;
    }

    console.log(`[mimo-agent] Received ${sessions.length} session(s)`);
    const sessionIds: string[] = [];

    for (const session of sessions) {
      const { sessionId, port, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword, acpSessionId } = session;

      try {
        const checkoutPath = join(this.config.workDir, sessionId);
        const platformHost = platformUrl
          .replace(/^https?:\/\//, "")
          .replace(/\/+$/, "");
        const fossilUrl = `http://${platformHost.split(":")[0]}:${port}/`;

        // Setup checkout directory with credentials
        await this.setupCheckout(sessionId, checkoutPath, fossilUrl, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);

        // Create session with credentials
        const sessionInfo = await this.sessionManager.createSession(
          sessionId,
          fossilUrl,
          agentWorkspaceUser,
          agentWorkspacePassword
        );

        // Store acpSessionId for later use during ACP init
        if (acpSessionId) {
          this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpSessionId(sessionId, acpSessionId);
        }

        // Spawn ACP process
        this.spawnAcpProcess(sessionInfo);

        sessionIds.push(sessionId);
        console.log(`[mimo-agent] Session ${sessionId} ready`);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(
          `[mimo-agent] Failed to setup session ${sessionId}:`,
          error
        );
        this.send({
          type: "session_error",
          sessionId,
          error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        });
      }
    }

    this.send({
      type: "agent_sessions_ready",
      sessionIds,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
  }
oldString:   private async handleSessionReady(message: any): Promise<void> {

      return;

      const { sessionId, port, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword } = session;

      try {
        const checkoutPath = join(this.config.workDir, sessionId);
        const platformHost = platformUrl
          .replace(/^https?:\/\//, "")
          .replace(/\/+$/, "");
        const fossilUrl = `http://${platformHost.split(":")[0]}:${port}/`;

        // Setup checkout directory with credentials
        await this.setupCheckout(sessionId, checkoutPath, fossilUrl, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);

        // Create session with credentials
        const sessionInfo = await this.sessionManager.createSession(
          sessionId,
          fossilUrl,
          agentWorkspaceUser,
          agentWorkspacePassword
        );

8:   onSessionError: (sessionId: string, error: string) => void;
9: }

14:   private changeTimeouts: Map<string, NodeJS.Timeout> = new Map();

19:     this.workDir = workDir;
20:     this.callbacks = callbacks;
21:   }

23:   getSession(sessionId: string): SessionInfo | undefined {
24:     return this.sessions.get(sessionId);
25:   }

28:     return Array.from(this.sessions.values());
29:   }

32:     sessionId: string,
33:     fossilUrl: string,
34:     fossilUser?: string,
35:     fossilPassword?: string
36:   ): Promise<SessionInfo> {
37:     const checkoutPath = join(this.workDir, sessionId);
38: 
39:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Creating session ${sessionId}`);
40:     console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Fossil URL: ${fossilUrl}`);
41:     console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Checkout: ${checkoutPath}`);
42: 
43:     // Clone/checkout logic handled by platform via fossil server
44:     // Just ensure the checkout directory exists
45:     if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
46:       mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
47:     }
48: 
49:     const sessionInfo: SessionInfo = {
50:       sessionId,
51:       checkoutPath,
52:       fossilUrl,
53:       fossilUser,
54:       fossilPassword,
55:       acpProcess: null,
56:       fileWatcher: null,
57:     };
58: 
59:     this.sessions.set(sessionId, sessionInfo);
60: 
61:     // Start file watcher
62:     this.startFileWatcher(sessionId, checkoutPath);
63: 
64:     return sessionInfo;
65:   }
66: 
67:   setSessionAcpProcess(sessionId: string, process: any): void {
68:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
69:     if (session) {
70:       session.acpProcess = process;
71:     }
72:   }
73: 
74:   setSessionState(
75:     sessionId: string,
76:     modelState?: ModelState,
77:     modeState?: ModeState
78:   ): void {
79:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
80:     if (session) {
81:       session.modelState = modelState;
82:       session.modeState = modeState;
83:     }
84:   }
85: 
86:   private startFileWatcher(sessionId: string, checkoutPath: string): void {
87:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Starting file watcher for session ${sessionId}`);
88: 
89:     const watcher = watch(
90:       checkoutPath,
91:       { recursive: true },
92:       (eventType: string, filename: string | null) => {
93:         if (!filename) return;
94: 
95:         // Skip hidden files and common ignore patterns
96:         if (
97:           filename.startsWith(".") ||
98:           filename.includes("/.") ||
99:           filename.includes("node_modules") ||
100:           filename.includes("__pycache__") ||
101:           filename.endsWith(".tmp") ||
102:           filename.endsWith("~")
103:         ) {
104:           return;
105:         }
106: 
107:         const change: FileChange = {
108:           path: filename,
109:           isNew: eventType === "rename",
110:           deleted: false,
111:         };
112: 
113:         const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId) || [];
114:         changes.push(change);
115:         this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, changes);
116: 
117:         const existingTimeout = this.changeTimeouts.get(sessionId);
118:         if (existingTimeout) {
119:           clearTimeout(existingTimeout);
120:         }
121: 
122:         const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
123:           this.flushPendingChanges(sessionId);
124:         }, 500);
125:         this.changeTimeouts.set(sessionId, timeout);
126:       }
127:     );
128: 
129:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
130:     if (session) {
131:       session.fileWatcher = watcher;
132:     }
133:   }
134: 
135:   private flushPendingChanges(sessionId: string): void {
136:     const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId);
137:     if (!changes || changes.length === 0) return;
138: 
139:     this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);
140:     this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);
141: 
142:     // Deduplicate changes
143:     const uniqueChanges = new Map<string, FileChange>();
144:     for (const change of changes) {
145:       uniqueChanges.set(change.path, change);
146:     }
147: 
148:     this.callbacks.onFileChange(
149:       sessionId,
150:       Array.from(uniqueChanges.values())
151:     );
152:   }
153: 
154:   terminateSession(sessionId: string): void {
155:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
156:     if (!session) return;
157: 
158:     if (session.acpProcess) {
159:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Killing ACP process for ${sessionId}`);
160:       session.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
161:     }
162: 
163:     if (session.fileWatcher) {
164:       session.fileWatcher.close();
165:     }
166: 
167:     // Clear any pending changes
168:     const timeout = this.changeTimeouts.get(sessionId);
169:     if (timeout) {
170:       clearTimeout(timeout);
171:       this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);
172:     }
173:     this.pendingChanges.delete(sessionId);
174: 
175:     this.sessions.delete(sessionId);
176:   }
177: 
178:   terminateAll(): void {
179:     for (const sessionId of this.sessions.keys()) {
180:       this.terminateSession(sessionId);
181:     }
182:   }
183: }

(End of file - total 183 lines)
</content>
```

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/test/agent-handoff.test.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:16:48

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/test/agent-handoff.test.ts
newString:   describe("session_ready message format", () => {
    it("should format session_ready with platformUrl and sessions", () => {
      const platformUrl = "http://localhost:3000";
      const sessions = [
        { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080 },
        { sessionId: "session-2", port: 8081 },
      ];

      const message = {
        type: "session_ready",
        platformUrl,
        sessions,
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("session_ready");
      expect(message.platformUrl).toBe("http://localhost:3000");
      expect(message.sessions).toHaveLength(2);
      expect(message.sessions[0].sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.sessions[0].port).toBe(8080);
    });

    it("should include acpSessionId when session has persisted ACP session", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
    });

    it("should send null acpSessionId when session has no persisted ACP session", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: null },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBeNull();
    });

    it("should handle mixed sessions with and without acpSessionId", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" },
          { sessionId: "session-2", port: 8081, acpSessionId: null },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
      expect(message.sessions[1].acpSessionId).toBeNull();
    });
  });
oldString:   describe("session_ready message format", () => {
    it("should format session_ready with platformUrl and sessions", () => {
      const platformUrl = "http://localhost:3000";
      const sessions = [
        { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080 },
        { sessionId: "session-2", port: 8081 },
      ];

      const message = {
        type: "session_ready",
        platformUrl,
        sessions,
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("session_ready");
      expect(message.platformUrl).toBe("http://localhost:3000");
      expect(message.sessions).toHaveLength(2);
      expect(message.sessions[0].sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.sessions[0].port).toBe(8080);
    });

    it("should handle empty sessions array", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready",
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [],
      };

      expect(message.sessions).toHaveLength(0);
    });

    it("should include all required fields per session", () => {
      const session = {
        sessionId: "test-session",
        port: 8080,
      };

      expect(session.sessionId).toBeDefined();
      expect(session.port).toBeDefined();
      expect(typeof session.sessionId).toBe("string");
      expect(typeof session.port).toBe("number");
    });
  });

newString:   describe("session_ready message format", () => {
    it("should format session_ready with platformUrl and sessions", () => {
      const platformUrl = "http://localhost:3000";
      const sessions = [
        { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080 },
        { sessionId: "session-2", port: 8081 },
      ];

      const message = {
        type: "session_ready",
        platformUrl,
        sessions,
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("session_ready");
      expect(message.platformUrl).toBe("http://localhost:3000");
      expect(message.sessions).toHaveLength(2);
      expect(message.sessions[0].sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.sessions[0].port).toBe(8080);
    });

    it("should include acpSessionId when session has persisted ACP session", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
    });

    it("should send null acpSessionId when session has no persisted ACP session", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: null },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBeNull();
    });

    it("should handle mixed sessions with and without acpSessionId", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "session_ready" as const,
        platformUrl: "http://localhost:3000",
        sessions: [
          { sessionId: "session-1", port: 8080, acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" },
          { sessionId: "session-2", port: 8081, acpSessionId: null },
        ],
      };

      expect(message.sessions[0].acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
      expect(message.sessions[1].acpSessionId).toBeNull();
    });
  });

  describe("acp_session_created message format", () => {
    it("should format acp_session_created with session resumption", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "acp_session_created" as const,
        sessionId: "session-1",
        acpSessionId: "acp-abc123",
        wasReset: false,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("acp_session_created");
      expect(message.sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
      expect(message.wasReset).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should format acp_session_created with session reset", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "acp_session_created" as const,
        sessionId: "session-1",
        acpSessionId: "acp-xyz789",
        wasReset: true,
        resetReason: "loadSession not supported",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("acp_session_created");
      expect(message.sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.acpSessionId).toBe("acp-xyz789");
      expect(message.wasReset).toBe(true);
      expect(message.resetReason).toBe("loadSession not supported");
    });

    it("should format acp_session_created with reset but no reason", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "acp_session_created" as const,
        sessionId: "session-1",
        acpSessionId: "acp-new456",
        wasReset: true,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      expect(message.wasReset).toBe(true);
      expect(message.resetReason).toBeUndefined();
    });
  });

  describe("System message format for session reset", () => {
    it("should format reset message with reason", () => {
      const timestamp = "2026-04-07T15:30:45.000Z";
      const reason = "loadSession not supported";
      const systemMessage = `Session reset at ${timestamp} (${reason})`;

      expect(systemMessage).toContain("Session reset at");
      expect(systemMessage).toContain(timestamp);
      expect(systemMessage).toContain(reason);
    });

    it("should format reset message without reason", () => {
      const timestamp = "2026-04-07T15:30:45.000Z";
      const systemMessage = `Session reset at ${timestamp}`;

      expect(systemMessage).toContain("Session reset at");
      expect(systemMessage).toContain(timestamp);
    });
  });

+    it("should format reset message without reason", () => {
+      const timestamp = "2026-04-07T15:30:45.000Z";
+      const systemMessage = `Session reset at ${timestamp}`;
+
+      expect(systemMessage).toContain("Session reset at");
+      expect(systemMessage).toContain(timestamp);
+    });
   });

  describe("ACP Session Resumption Messages", () => {
    it("should format InitializeResult with successful resumption", () => {
      const result = {
        acpSessionId: "acp-abc123",
        wasReset: false,
      };

      expect(result.acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
      expect(result.wasReset).toBe(false);
      expect(result.resetReason).toBeUndefined();
    });

    it("should format InitializeResult with reset due to capability", () => {
      const result = {
        acpSessionId: "acp-xyz789",
        wasReset: true,
        resetReason: "loadSession not supported",
      };

      expect(result.acpSessionId).toBe("acp-xyz789");
      expect(result.wasReset).toBe(true);
      expect(result.resetReason).toBe("loadSession not supported");
    });

    it("should format InitializeResult with reset due to error", () => {
      const result = {
        acpSessionId: "acp-new456",
        wasReset: true,
        resetReason: "loadSession failed",
      };

      expect(result.wasReset).toBe(true);
      expect(result.resetReason).toBe("loadSession failed");
    });

    it("should format acp_session_created for successful resumption", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "acp_session_created",
        sessionId: "session-1",
        acpSessionId: "acp-abc123",
        wasReset: false,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("acp_session_created");
      expect(message.sessionId).toBe("session-1");
      expect(message.acpSessionId).toBe("acp-abc123");
      expect(message.wasReset).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should format acp_session_created for reset with reason", () => {
      const message = {
        type: "acp_session_created",
        sessionId: "session-1",
        acpSessionId: "acp-xyz789",
        wasReset: true,
        resetReason: "loadSession not supported",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };

      expect(message.type).toBe("acp_session_created");
      expect(message.wasReset).toBe(true);
      expect(message.resetReason).toBe("loadSession not supported");
    });
  });

  describe("Capability detection", () => {
    it("should treat undefined loadSession as false", () => {
      const capabilities = {
        loadSession: undefined,
      };

      const hasLoadSession = capabilities.loadSession ?? false;
      expect(hasLoadSession).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should treat explicit false loadSession as false", () => {
      const capabilities = {
        loadSession: false,
      };

      expect(capabilities.loadSession).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should recognize true loadSession capability", () => {
      const capabilities = {
        loadSession: true,
      };

      expect(capabilities.loadSession).toBe(true);
    });
  });
